Telescope location in the field (TLLOC) the parameters are:
   -the telescope identification number 
   -the X (oriented towrd east) location cordinate in meters. 
   -the Y (oriented toward north)location cordinate in meters. 
   -the Z (oriented toward up) location cordinate in meters. 
   -the telescope rotation offset in meters.
    The telescope rotation offset is the distance below the focal point
        of the mirror along the optical axis about which the telescope
        rotates. (intersection of the elevation and azimuth axis)
   -the pointing offset in the x direction
   -the pointing offset in the y direction

coordinates August 2006, origin in array center for old array (origin offset 
for new array!)
Z coordinates set to zero for compatibility with Corsika; may want nonzero 
values with full grisu chain.
 TLLOC 1     -37.6 -23.7 5 12.0 0.0 0.0
* TLLOC 1     135.48 -8.61 5 12.0 0.0 0.0

Elisa: FADCSAMPLINGWIDTH 0 1. I think only first number is used
The simulation parameter record SIMUL contains
   -the time between samples in ns (this is also the sampling time 
    for the simulation calculation to be carried with.)
   -the number of samples over which the simulation produces the signals
   2) changed readout window from 20 to 16
   -the number of samples over which the noise database is produced
(GM) should be 20000, but noise calculation currently extremly slow
* SIMUL 1.0 100 4000

The FADC record (FADC) contains
   -the FADC output ON-OFF status  (1=ON, 0=OFF) Elisa: not used
   -the FADC output voltage per digital count in mV: Elisa: not used
   -the FADC pedestal in digital counts Elisa: think this is used - why don't FADCSAMPLES & FADCHIGHGAINPEDESTAL match?
   -the FADC digital output dynamic range Elisa: think this is used FADCDYNAMICRANGE
   -the number of sample to be written on the output for each channel. Elisa: check VCameraRed
   -the number of samples between the trigger and the beginning of the
    FADC record. A positive number corresponds to a record starting
    at a time anterior to the trigger time. Elisa: not used
   -the number of samples in pedestal event records Elisa: not used
   -The ratio between high and low gain for system with hi-lo gain switch
    dynamic range extention. If this number is less than 1.0 the function 
    is disabled. Elisa: used FADCLOHIGHGAINRATIO?
   -The threshold in FADCdigital counts for the low gain activation. Elisa: used FADCHILOGAINTHRESHOLD

(GM) noise length should be 20000, but noise calculation currently extremly slow

Pattern Selection trigger (PSTON).
   -the minimum number of adjacent triggered channels required by the 
    pattern trigger logic
   -the number of 19 pixel trigger patches Elisa: only last number used-> not sure how to get this, but doesn't appear to be used further in code
* PSTON 3 91

Elisa: don't think we have this for SCT: USETRIGGERSUBFIELDS 0 0
Trigger patch list records (PATCH)
   -Patch identification number 
   -A flag indicating if the patch is enabled (1) or not (0).
   -List of id numbers for pixels in patch (0 indicates no pixel connected)
    The order of the 19 pixel list is important.
(GM) corrected patch 33 here, was wrong in originately distributed configuration file

 PATCH 1 1   12  13  14  15  16 11    4   5   6  17  10   3   1   7  18   9   2  19   8

Mirror design (MIROR). The parameters are 
   -the telescope identification number
   -the mirror radius in meters Elisa: I am not sure what to put here, outer radius of primary (PRIMARY)? check how this is used - only used in VDisplayBirdsEye
   -focal length in meters Elisa: TELESCOPEFOCALLENGTH
   -the focusing error in meters (>0 when camera is too 
    far away from the dish)
   -the mirror type (1=DavisCotton) Elisa: not used 
   -the number of mirror elements. Elisa: not used

* MIROR 1 4.8319 5.5863 0. 1 357

   -the number of phototubes. Elisa: only this used, but there is another value in the CARE config file

Phototubes (PMPIX).  
   -the telescope identification number Used
   -the pixel identification number Used
   -the pixel shape (1=circular, 2=hexagonal, 3=square) Not used?
   -orientation angle(degrees). If 0.0, polygon side perpendicular
    to the y-axis Not used?
   -the X position coordinate in the focal plane in mm Used
   -the Y position coordinate in the focal plane in mm Used
    Camera coordinates are such that increasing X corresponds to 
    going WEST when telescope is pointing SOUTH. Increasing Y 
    corresponds to increasing elevation.
   -the PMT Radius in mm Used
    The PMT radius really is the radius of the sensitive area (Radius of 
    the light cone input for example). 
   -the geometrical efficiency which may be used to include the effects 
    of light cone loss. Not used
   -the quantum efficiency identification number to be used for that tube. Not used
   -the single photoelectron signal relative amplitude fluctuation. Not used
   -the signal rize time in nanosecondes Not used
   -the signal fall time  in nanosecondes Not used
   -the RC coupling time constant in nanosecondes Not used
   -the bellongin of the channel to the trigger (1 if it bellongs, 
    0 other wise) Used
   -a flag indicating if the pixel should be used in the analysis(1) or not(0) Used
   -a time offset in nanosecond. It measures how late the pulse is locate in 
       the stack for each channel. the analysis and the simulation search 
       for the smalles non negative value and subtract it from all the other 
       to apply a relative correction. Used
   -a relative gain factor to account for the imperfect gain flat fielding. Used
    In the anlysis, each pixel value is multiplied by this number while 
    in the simulation pulse amplitudes are divided by this number.
